  R8_UNIFORM_01 samples a uniform random
  distribution in [0,1].

  Starting with seed =    123456789

  First few values:

         1    0.218418    
         2    0.956318    
         3    0.829509    
         4    0.561695    
         5    0.415307    

  Number of values computed was N =     1000
  Average value was   0.503040    
  Minimum value was   0.183837E-02
  Maximum value was   0.997908    
  Variance was   0.822497E-01

  For converting between Julian Ephemeris Dates
  and Mayan Long Count dates:
  JED_TO_MAYAN_LONG,
  MAYAN_LONG_TO_JED.
 
  JED (in)       MAYAN			   JED (out)
                 P   B   K   T   U   D

TEST46
  For the current time and date, "NOW", 
  NOW_TO_JED returns the JED,
  NOW_TO_YJF_COMMON the YJF date,
  NOW_TO_YMDF_COMMON returns the YMDF date,
  NOW_TO_YMDHMS_COMMON the YMDHMS date.
 
 
  FORTRAN90 DATE_AND_TIME routine says:
    Now is 20200608 154241.868
 
  NOW_TO_JED_COMMON:    Now is:  2459009.15
  NOW_TO_YJF_COMMON:     Now is: CE 2020/160.65
  NOW_TO_YMDF_COMMON:    Now is: CE 2020/06/08.65
  NOW_TO_YMDHMS_COMMON: Now is: CE 2020/06/08 15:42:41

TEST70
  For the Common calendar:
  YMDF_INC_COMMON increments a date by days;
  YMDF_NEXT_COMMON computes the next day,
  YMDF_PREV_COMMON computes the previous day.

TEST75
  For the Common calendar,
  YMD_INC_YMD_COMMON increments a YMDF date by YMDF;
  YMDF_DIF_YMDF_COMMON finds the YMDF difference.
 
 
    Date1        increment    Date2          difference
 
  CE 1900/05/27.00       50  9 10  CE 1951/03/09.00       50  9 10
